UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F18 = (select (case when 2*isnull(f12,0)-isnull(f5,0)>0 then 2*isnull(f12,0)-isnull(f5,0) else 0 end)*F100.F100973 from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003  
where an=2019 and Luna=12 and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = 307) WHERE F10003=307 AND "An"=2019 AND "Luna"=12;
UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F19 = (select isnull(F5,0) - ((isnull(F12,0)*2) - isnull(F18,0)/F100.F100973) from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
where an=2019 and Luna=12 and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = 307) WHERE F10003=307 AND "An"=2019 AND "Luna"=12;
UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F20 = (select (case when isnull(f11,0)-isnull(f19,0)>0 then isnull(f11,0)-isnull(f19,0) else 0 end)*F100.F100973 
from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003

UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F22 = (Select (isnull(F5,0)-isnull(F19,0))/2 from Ptj_Cumulat

UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F23 = ( SELECT Ramase FROM SituatieZileAbsente WHERE F10003=307 AND An=YEAR(ent.DataInceput)) WHERE F10003=307 AND "An"=2019 AND "Luna"=12;
UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F43 = (select   f30 - cast (case when isnull(F100.F10043,0)=0 then  isnull(F15,0)/8  else   isnull(F11,0) /F100.F10043 end as int) - isnull(F1,0) - isnull(F2,0) - isnull(F3,0)
- isnull(F4,0)
- isnull(F6,0)
 from  ptj_cumulat inner join F100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
  where an=2019 and Luna=12 and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = 307) WHERE F10003=307 AND "An"=2019 AND "Luna"=12;
UPDATE "Ptj_Cumulat" SET F30 = (select sum (case when  zilibera >0 or  ZiLiberaLegala > 0  then 0 else 1 end) from ptj_intrari
join f100 on ptj_intrari.f10003 = f100.f10003 and cast(ziua as date) between f10022 and f10023
 where year(Ziua)=2019 AND MONTH(Ziua)=12 AND Ptj_intrari.F10003=307) WHERE F10003=307 AND "An"=2019 AND "Luna"=12;

END;

                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F100893,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Et. ' + a.F100893 END) +

                            (CASE WHEN a.F100897 is null or a.F100897 = 0 THEN '' ELSE case when niv3.tip in (11, 19, 22, 23) then ' sat ' + niv3.denloc else
                            case when niv3.tip = 6 and upper(niv3.denloc) not like '%SECTOR%' then ' sector ' + niv3.DENLOC else ' ' + niv3.denloc end END end) +

                            (case when a.F100914 is null or a.F100914 = 0 THEN '' else case when niv2.tip in (1, 4) and UPPER(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%MUNICIPIU%' then ' municipiul ' + niv2.DENLOC else
                            case when niv2.tip = 2 and UPPER(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%ORAS%' then ' orasul ' + niv2.DENLOC else 
                            case when niv2.TIP = 3 and upper(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%COMUNA%' then ' comuna ' + niv2.DENLOC else ' ' + niv2.denloc end end end end ) +

                            (CASE WHEN a.F100921 is null or a.F100921 = 0 THEN '' ELSE case when upper(niv1.denloc) like '%JUDET%' or upper(niv1.denloc)  like '%MUNICIPIU%' then ' ' + niv1.DENLOC else
                             case when upper(niv1.denloc) like '%BUCURESTI%' then ' municipiul ' + niv1.DENLOC else ' judetul ' + niv1.denloc end end END) +
                            

                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10087,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Cod Postal. ' + a.F10087 END) AS "AdresaCompleta"
                             
                            FROM F100 A
                            LEFT JOIN F002 E ON A.F10002 = E.F00202 
                            LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304 
                            LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405 
                            LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506 
                            LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607 
                            left join Localitati niv1 on niv1.SIRUTA = a.F100921
                            left join Localitati niv2 on niv2.SIRUTA = a.F100914
                            left join Localitati niv3 on niv3.SIRUTA = a.F100897
                             
                            WHERE 1=1  AND A.F10003 IN (SELECT CAST(F10003 AS INT) AS F10003 FROM USERS WHERE F70102 = 2
                            UNION
                            SELECT B.F10003 FROM "relGrupAngajat" B
                            INNER JOIN "MP_relGrupSuper" C ON B."IdGrup" = C."IdGrup"
                             inner join f100 e on b.F10003=e.F10003 
                            WHERE C."IdSuper" = 2  AND ( OR  OR  OR  OR  OR )
                            UNION
                            SELECT CAST(B.F10003 AS INT) AS F10003 FROM "relGrupAngajat" B
                            INNER JOIN "MP_relGrupSuper" C ON B."IdGrup" = C."IdGrup"
                            INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" D ON B.F10003=D.F10003 AND C."IdSuper" = -1 * D."IdSuper"
                             inner join f100 e on b.F10003=e.F10003 
                            WHERE D."IdUser" = 2  AND ( OR  OR  OR  OR  OR ))
                            ) X WHERE 1=1  AND ( "Stare"='Active' OR  "Stare"='Actively suspended' OR  "Stare"='Inactive' OR  "Stare"='Candidate' OR  "Stare"='Engaged in advance' OR  "Stare"='Active detached')
                            ORDER BY "NumeComplet"

                                1 AS "IdCircuit", "IdSuper", 
                                CASE WHEN (0 = 1) AND ((CONVERT(int,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT 1)))) = 1) THEN 4 ELSE 
                                (CASE WHEN "Total" = 1 THEN 3 ELSE 
                                (CASE WHEN "Total" = (CONVERT(int,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT 1)))) THEN 3 ELSE
                                (CASE WHEN ((CONVERT(int,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT 1)))) = 1) THEN 1 ELSE 2 END) END) END) END AS "IdStare", 
                                "IdUser", 
                                CONVERT(int,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT 1))) AS Pozitie, 
                                CASE WHEN (0 = 1) THEN (CASE WHEN (CONVERT(int,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT 1)))) = 1 THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) ELSE (CASE WHEN "IdUser" = 3 THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) END AS "Aprobat", 
                                CASE WHEN (0 = 1) THEN (CASE WHEN (CONVERT(int,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT 1)))) = 1 THEN GetDate() ELSE NULL END) ELSE (CASE WHEN "IdUser" = 3 THEN GetDate() ELSE NULL END) END AS "DataAprobare", 
                                3 AS USER_NO, GetDate() AS TIME, 0 AS "Inlocuitor", NULL AS "IdUserInlocuitor" 
                                FROM (SELECT W.*, COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY 1) AS "Total" FROM ( SELECT TOP 1 0 AS "Index", IdUser, -3 AS IdSuper, 0 AS "Inlocuitor" FROM (
                                        SELECT TOP 1 IdUser FROM F100Supervizori WHERE F10003 = 17 AND IdSuper = (-1 * -3) AND IdUser = 3
                                        UNION ALL
                                        SELECT TOP 1 IdUser FROM F100Supervizori WHERE F10003 = 17 AND IdSuper = (-1 * -3)
                                        ) x ) W) X) G; INSERT INTO "Ptj_Cereri"("Id", F10003, "IdAbsenta", "DataInceput", "DataSfarsit", "NrZile", "NrZileViitor", "Observatii", "IdStare", "IdCircuit", "UserIntrod", "Culoare", "Inlocuitor", "TotalSuperCircuit", "Pozitie", "TrimiteLa", "NrOre", "AreAtas", "CampExtra1", "CampExtra2", "CampExtra3", "CampExtra4", "CampExtra5", "CampExtra6", "CampExtra7", "CampExtra8", "CampExtra9", "CampExtra10", "CampExtra11", "CampExtra12", "CampExtra13", "CampExtra14", "CampExtra15", "CampExtra16", "CampExtra17", "CampExtra18", "CampExtra19", "CampExtra20")

                        SELECT A.F10003, 0 AS "Rol", COALESCE((SELECT COALESCE("Alias", "Denumire") FROM "tblSupervizori" WHERE "Id"=0),'Angajat') AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        WHERE A.F10003 = 
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, B."IdSuper" AS "Rol", CASE WHEN D."Alias" IS NOT NULL AND D."Alias" <> '' THEN D."Alias" ELSE D."Denumire" END AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        INNER JOIN "Ptj_Circuit" C ON B."IdSuper" = -1 * c."UserIntrod" 
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= 
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, 76 AS "Rol", 'Fara rol' AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "Ptj_Circuit" C ON C."UserIntrod"= ) B
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F718 X ON A.F10071=X.F71802
                        LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304
                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405
                        LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506
                        LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607
                        WHERE 1=1

Eroarea:   SELECT B."Rol", B.F10003, A.F10008 + ' ' + A.F10009 AS "NumeComplet", A.F10017 AS CNP, A.F10022 AS "DataAngajarii", A.F10023 AS "DataPlecarii",
                        A.F10011 AS "NrContract", CAST(A.F10043 AS int) AS "Norma",A.F100901, CASE WHEN (A.F10025 = 0 OR A.F10025=999) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS "AngajatActiv",
                        X.F71804 AS "Functia", F.F00305 AS "Subcompanie",G.F00406 AS "Filiala",H.F00507 AS "Sectie",I.F00608 AS "Departament", B."RolDenumire"  
                        FROM (
                        SELECT A.F10003, 0 AS "Rol", COALESCE((SELECT COALESCE("Alias", "Denumire") FROM "tblSupervizori" WHERE "Id"=0),'Angajat') AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        WHERE A.F10003 = 
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, B."IdSuper" AS "Rol", CASE WHEN D."Alias" IS NOT NULL AND D."Alias" <> '' THEN D."Alias" ELSE D."Denumire" END AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        INNER JOIN "Ptj_Circuit" C ON B."IdSuper" = -1 * c."UserIntrod" 
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= 
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, 76 AS "Rol", 'Fara rol' AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "Ptj_Circuit" C ON C."UserIntrod"= ) B
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F718 X ON A.F10071=X.F71802
                        LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304
                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405
                        LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506
                        LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607
                        WHERE 1=1

                                2 AS USER_NO, GetDate() AS TIME,

                                CASE WHEN (SELECT MAX("IdCentruCost") FROM "F100CentreCost" C WHERE C.F10003 = B.F10003 AND C."DataInceput" <= A.Zi AND  A.Zi <= C."DataSfarsit") IS NULL THEN 
                                CASE WHEN COALESCE(dc.CC, 9999) <> 9999 THEN dc.CC ELSE (SELECT C.F00615 FROM F006 C WHERE C.F00607 = dd.Dept) END 
                                ELSE (SELECT MAX("IdCentruCost") FROM "F100CentreCost" C WHERE C.F10003 = B.F10003 AND C."DataInceput" <=  A.Zi AND  A.Zi <= C."DataSfarsit") END AS "F06204Default",
                                CASE WHEN (CASE WHEN C.DAY is not null THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) = 1 AND Y."TipSchimb8" = 1 THEN  COALESCE(Y."Program8", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE
                                CASE (CASE WHEN datepart(dw,A."Zi") - 1 = 0 THEN 7 ELSE datepart(dw,A.Zi) - 1 END)
                                WHEN 1 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb1",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program1", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                WHEN 2 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb2",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program2", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                WHEN 3 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb3",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program3", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                WHEN 4 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb4",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program4", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                WHEN 5 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb5",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program5", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                WHEN 6 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb6",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program6", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                WHEN 7 THEN (CASE WHEN COALESCE(Y."TipSchimb7",1) = 1 THEN COALESCE(Y."Program7", Y."Program0", -99) ELSE -99 END) 
                                END END AS "IdProgram"

                                FROM "tblZile" A
                                INNER JOIN F100 B ON 1=1 AND B.F10022 <= CONVERT(date,A."Zi")  AND CONVERT(date,A."Zi")  <= B.F10023
                                LEFT JOIN HOLIDAYS C on A."Zi"=C.DAY
                                LEFT JOIN (SELECT X.F10003, X."Ziua", COUNT(*) AS CNT FROM "Ptj_Intrari" X WHERE YEAR(X."Ziua")=2020 AND MONTH(X."Ziua")=1 GROUP BY X.F10003, X."Ziua") D ON D.F10003=B.F10003 AND D."Ziua" = A."Zi"
                                LEFT JOIN DamiNorma_Table dn ON dn.F10003=B.F10003 AND dn.dt=A.Zi
                                LEFT JOIN DamiCC_Table     dc ON dc.F10003=B.F10003 AND dc.dt=A.Zi
								LEFT JOIN DamiDept_Table   dd ON dd.F10003=B.F10003 AND dd.dt=A.Zi                                
                                LEFT JOIN F006 G ON G.F00607 = dd.Dept
                                LEFT JOIN "Ptj_Contracte" Y ON Y."Id"=(SELECT MAX("IdContract") FROM "F100Contracte" BB WHERE BB.F10003 = B.F10003 AND BB."DataInceput" <= A.Zi AND A.Zi <= BB."DataSfarsit")
                                WHERE YEAR(A."Zi")=2020 AND MONTH(A."Zi")=1 AND COALESCE(D.CNT,0) = 0;
